  z-index: 900;
}

}

<!-- custom JS -->
<script>

  requirejs.config( {
    "paths": {
      "tween": "https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/gsap/1.19.1/TweenMax.min"
    },
    "shim": {
      "tween": {
        "deps": ["jquery"], "exports": "TweenMax"
      }
    }
  });

  require(['tween'], function() {

    $(document).ready(function(){

      var $obj = $(".modal"),
          $dObj = $("#dynamicModal"),
          $overlay = $(".modal-overlay");

      function getPos() {
        return $obj.position();
      }

      var lastPos = getPos();

      function update() {
        var pos = getPos();
        var limit = 20;
        var dx = Math.min(limit, Math.abs(pos.left - lastPos.left) * 0.5);
        var dy = Math.min(limit, Math.abs(pos.top - lastPos.top) * 0.5);
        // setBlur(dx+","+dy);

        lastPos = pos;
        requestAnimationFrame(update);
      }

      update();

      var isOpen = false;

      function openModal() {
        /*$overlay.css({
          display:"block"
        })*/
        TweenMax.to($overlay, 0.1, {autoAlpha: 1});

        TweenMax.fromTo($obj, .75, {y: -($(document).height() + $dObj.height())}, {
          delay: 0.15,
          y: "0%",
          ease: Power2.easeIn
        });
      }

      function closeModal() {
        TweenMax.to($overlay, 0.1, {delay: 0.55, autoAlpha: 0});
        TweenMax.to($obj, 0.55, {y: -($(document).height() + $dObj.height()), ease: Back.easeIn});
      }

      $(".open-modal").click(function () {
        openModal();
      })
      $(".close-modal,.modal-overlay").click(function () {
        closeModal();
      })


      function sendMyAjax(URL_address){

        $('body').on('click touchstart', '.promo-detail-btn', function(e){
          // AJAX calls to dynamic url
          var URL_address = $(this).attr('data-page') + '.html';
          var jaxed = $(this).attr('data-loaded-content');
          var dynamicClass = $(this).attr('data-loaded-class');

          openModal();
          $('.modal').css('min-height', '245px');
          $.ajax({
            url: URL_address,
            dataType: 'html',
            cache: false, // cache to false helps function on mobile
            beforeSend: function(){
            },
            success: function(data){
              var div =  $(data).find(jaxed);
              $('.dynamic-content').html(div);
              $('#loadPromo').css('visibility', 'hidden');
            }
          });
        });
      }; // end AJAX function

      $('.promo-detail-btn').click(sendMyAjax); // load content via AJAX function

    });
  });// end require call for tween

</script>
